In case parameter \char`\"{}(heading)\char`\"{} is the empty \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a13690c1a2aacb1c8261e3be3c4a4f4b2}{string}} no heading is generated. \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}anchor This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} places an invisible, named anchor \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}cite Adds \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} bibliographic reference in the text \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} in the list of bibliographic references. The \textbackslash{}$<$ label\textbackslash{}$>$ must \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} valid Bib\+TeX label that can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} found in one of the .bib files listed in \textbackslash{}ref cfg\+\_\+cite\+\_\+bib\+\_\+files \char`\"{}C\+I\+T\+E\+\_\+\+B\+I\+B\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES\char`\"{}. For the \textbackslash{}La\+TeX \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad41edd103217aafc3fb5613fe98b87a0}{output}} the formatting of the reference in the text can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} configured with \textbackslash{}ref cfg\+\_\+latex\+\_\+bib\+\_\+style \char`\"{}L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+B\+I\+B\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+LE\char`\"{}. For other \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad41edd103217aafc3fb5613fe98b87a0}{output}} formats \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} fixed representation is used. Note that using \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad61af623360700a24d0f4b7682a029fb}{this}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} requires the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} bibtex tool to \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} present in the \mbox{\hyperlink{search__functions_8php_af66786bda8b625ad1ea9c3e8adf0862f}{search}} path.$<$ hr $>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdendlink \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endlink \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endlink This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} ends \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} link that is started with the \textbackslash{}ref cmdlink \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}link\char`\"{} command. \textbackslash{}sa section \textbackslash{}ref cmdlink \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}link\char`\"{}.$<$ hr $>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdlink \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}link$<$ link-\/object $>$ \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}link The links that \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a8ed5a546d1a76d96eeab1587ee2de2c1}{are}} automatically generated by doxygen always have the name of the object they point to as link-\/text. The \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}link \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to create \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} link to an object(\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}}, class, or member) with \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} user specified link-\/text. The link \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} should end with an \textbackslash{}ref cmdendlink \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endlink\char`\"{} command. All text between the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}link \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \textbackslash{}ref cmdendlink \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endlink\char`\"{} commands serves as text for \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} link to the \textbackslash{}$<$ link-\/object\textbackslash{}$>$ specified as the first argument of \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}link. \textbackslash{}sa Section \textbackslash{}ref autolink \char`\"{}autolink\char`\"{} for more information on automatically generated links \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} valid link-\/objects.$<$ hr $>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdref \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ref$<$ name $>$\mbox{[}\char`\"{}(text)\char`\"{}\mbox{]} \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ref Creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} reference to \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} named section, subsection, page or anchor. For H\+T\+ML documentation the reference \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} will generate \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} link to the section. For \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} section or subsection the title of the section will \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used as the text of the link. For an anchor the optional text between quotes will \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used or \textbackslash{}$<$ name\textbackslash{}$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} no text is specified. For \textbackslash{}La\+TeX documentation the reference \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} will generate \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} section number for sections or the text followed by \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} page number \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} \textbackslash{}$<$ name\textbackslash{}$>$ refers to an anchor. \textbackslash{}sa Section \textbackslash{}ref cmdpage \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}page\char`\"{} for an example of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ref command.$<$ hr $>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdrefitem \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}refitem$<$ name $>$ \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}refitem Just like the \textbackslash{}ref cmdref \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ref\char`\"{} command, \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad61af623360700a24d0f4b7682a029fb}{this}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} reference to \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} named section, but \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad61af623360700a24d0f4b7682a029fb}{this}} reference appears in \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} list that is started by \textbackslash{}ref cmdsecreflist \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}secreflist\char`\"{} and ends with \textbackslash{}ref cmdendsecreflist \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endsecreflist\char`\"{}. An example of such \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} list can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} seen \textbackslash{}ref showsecreflist \char`\"{}at the top of the page\char`\"{}.$<$ hr $>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdsecreflist \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}secreflist \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}secreflist Starts an index list of item, created with \textbackslash{}ref cmdrefitem \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}refitem\char`\"{} that each link to \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} named section.$<$ hr $>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdendsecreflist \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endsecreflist \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endsecreflist \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2vhdlcode_8cpp_a342404d3b71fbd50588f779f1f1c59b3}{End}} an index list started with \textbackslash{}ref cmdsecreflist \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}secreflist\char`\"{}.$<$ hr $>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdsubpage \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subpage$<$ name $>$\mbox{[}\char`\"{}(text)\char`\"{}\mbox{]} \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subpage This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to create \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} hierarchy of pages. The same structure can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} made using the \textbackslash{}ref cmddefgroup \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}defgroup\char`\"{} and \textbackslash{}ref cmdingroup \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ingroup\char`\"{} commands, but for pages the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subpage \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} is often more convenient. The \mbox{\hyperlink{main_8cpp_ae66f6b31b5ad750f1fe042a706a4e3d4}{main}} page(see \textbackslash{}ref cmdmainpage \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}mainpage\char`\"{}) is typically the root of hierarchy. This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} behaves similar as \textbackslash{}ref cmdref \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ref\char`\"{} in the sense that it creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} reference to \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} page labeled \textbackslash{}$<$ name\textbackslash{}$>$ with the optional link text as specified in the second argument. It differs from the \textbackslash{}ref cmdref \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ref\char`\"{} command in that it only works for pages, \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} parent-\/child relation between pages, where the child page(or \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_acc128504834a67c06b246c155ca48807}{sub}} page) is identified by label \textbackslash{}$<$ name\textbackslash{}$>$. See the \textbackslash{}ref cmdsection \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}section\char`\"{} and \textbackslash{}ref cmdsubsection \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsection\char`\"{} commands \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} you want to \mbox{\hyperlink{restypedef_8cpp_a102acaaa258e937adf910898c6133545}{add}} structure without creating multiple pages. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad0ca7f287bf31aee006876639e63bfcb}{note}} Each page can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} the \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_acc128504834a67c06b246c155ca48807}{sub}} page of only one other page \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} no cyclic relations \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a8ed5a546d1a76d96eeab1587ee2de2c1}{are}} allowed, i.\+e. the page hierarchy must have \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} tree structure. Here is an example\+:\textbackslash{}verbatim \textbackslash{}endverbatim$<$ hr $>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdtableofcontents \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}tableofcontents\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}\{\textquotesingle{}\mbox{[}option\mbox{[}\+:\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}}\mbox{]}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}, option\mbox{[}\+:\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}}\mbox{]}\mbox{]} $\ast$\textquotesingle{}\}\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}tableofcontents Creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} table of contents at the top of \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} page, listing all sections \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} subsections in the page. The \`{}option\`{} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} \`{}H\+T\+ML\`{} or \`{}La\+TeX\`{} or \`{}X\+ML\`{} or \`{}Doc\+Book\`{}. When \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} \`{}\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}}\`{} is specified \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad61af623360700a24d0f4b7682a029fb}{this}} means the maximum nesting \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}} that is shown. The value of \`{}\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}}\`{} should \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} in the range 1..\+5, \mbox{\hyperlink{qtextcodec_8cpp_a48ca6217f9d5d1de9776060e1a8dbe58}{values}} outside \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad61af623360700a24d0f4b7682a029fb}{this}} range \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a8ed5a546d1a76d96eeab1587ee2de2c1}{are}} considered to \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} 5. In case no \`{}\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}}\`{} is specified \`{}\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}}\`{} is \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a71ce05caaf1d98a296e01c62ee8489b3}{set}} to 5(show all) In case no \`{}option\`{}. is specified \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}tableofcontents acts as \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} just the \`{}option\`{} \`{}H\+T\+ML\`{} \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \`{}X\+ML\`{} was specified. In case of multiple \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}tableofcontents commands in \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} page the \`{}option\`{}(\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a011c73f2dbb87635a3b4206c72355f6e}{s}}) will \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used additional to the already specified \`{}option\`{}(\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a011c73f2dbb87635a3b4206c72355f6e}{s}}), but only the last \`{}\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}}\`{} of an \`{}option\`{} is valid. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{qglobal_8h_ac3b81b0c037874b7fcfd69376a6d5594}{warning}} This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} only works inside related page documentation \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_aff65a51a703804e0ad1adbcfd76c86f8}{e}} not in other documentation blocks \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} only has effect in the the specified output!$<$ hr $>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdsection \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}section$<$ section-\/name $>$(section title) \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}section Creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} section with name \textbackslash{}$<$ section-\/name\textbackslash{}$>$. The title of the section should \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} specified as the second argument of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}section command. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{qglobal_8h_ac3b81b0c037874b7fcfd69376a6d5594}{warning}} This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} only works inside related page documentation \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_aff65a51a703804e0ad1adbcfd76c86f8}{e}} not in other documentation blocks! \textbackslash{}sa Section \textbackslash{}ref cmdpage \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}page\char`\"{} for an example of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}section command.$<$ hr $>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdsubsection \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsection$<$ subsection-\/name $>$(subsection title) \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsection Creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} subsection with name \textbackslash{}$<$ subsection-\/name\textbackslash{}$>$. The title of the subsection should \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} specified as the second argument of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsection command. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{qglobal_8h_ac3b81b0c037874b7fcfd69376a6d5594}{warning}} This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} only works inside \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} section of \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} related page documentation block \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_aff65a51a703804e0ad1adbcfd76c86f8}{e}} not in other documentation blocks! \textbackslash{}sa Section \textbackslash{}ref cmdpage \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}page\char`\"{} for an example of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsection command.$<$ hr $>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdsubsubsection \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsubsection$<$ subsubsection-\/name $>$(subsubsection title) \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsubsection Creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} subsubsection with name \textbackslash{}$<$ subsubsection-\/name\textbackslash{}$>$. The title of the subsubsection should \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} specified as the second argument of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsubsection command. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{qglobal_8h_ac3b81b0c037874b7fcfd69376a6d5594}{warning}} This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} only works inside \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} subsection of \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} related page documentation block \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_aff65a51a703804e0ad1adbcfd76c86f8}{e}} not in other documentation blocks! \textbackslash{}sa Section \textbackslash{}ref cmdpage \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}page\char`\"{} for an example of the \textbackslash{}ref cmdsection \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}section\char`\"{} command \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \textbackslash{}ref cmdsubsection \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsection\char`\"{} command.$<$ hr $>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdparagraph \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}}-\/name $>$(\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} title) \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} Creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} named \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} with name \textbackslash{}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}}-\/name\textbackslash{}$>$. The title of the \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} should \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} specified as the second argument of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} command. \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a15229b450f26d8fa1c10bea4f3279f4d}{p}} $>$\textbackslash{}endhtmlonly$<$ hr $>$ \textbackslash{}section cmddontinclude \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}dontinclude\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}\{lineno\}\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}}-\/name $>$ \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}dontinclude This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a8ac09b377c3e2343a4bf758132f67c22}{parse}} \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} source \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} without actually verbatim including it in the documentation(as the \textbackslash{}ref cmdinclude \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}include\char`\"{} command does). This is useful \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} you want to divide the source \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} into smaller pieces \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \mbox{\hyperlink{restypedef_8cpp_a102acaaa258e937adf910898c6133545}{add}} documentation between the pieces. Source files or directories can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} specified using the \textbackslash{}ref cfg\+\_\+example\+\_\+path \char`\"{}E\+X\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH\char`\"{} tag of doxygen \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a011c73f2dbb87635a3b4206c72355f6e}{s}} configuration file. You can \mbox{\hyperlink{restypedef_8cpp_a102acaaa258e937adf910898c6133545}{add}} option \`{}\{lineno\}\`{} to enable line numbers for the \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a327f3dad9da687756493417c1c902612}{included}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_a7ebb47cd48f4220dc255e5fea2063b89}{code}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} desired. The class \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} member declarations \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} definitions inside the \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_a7ebb47cd48f4220dc255e5fea2063b89}{code}} fragment \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a8ed5a546d1a76d96eeab1587ee2de2c1}{are}} \textquotesingle{}remembered\textquotesingle{} during the parsing of the \mbox{\hyperlink{vhdldocgen_8cpp_ae8c2c4e6dab650ca0dbc32956838ddd9}{comment}} block that contained the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}dontinclude command. For line by line descriptions of source files, one or more lines of the example can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} displayed using the \textbackslash{}ref cmdline \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}line\char`\"{}, \textbackslash{}ref cmdskip \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}skip\char`\"{}, \textbackslash{}ref cmdskipline \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}skipline\char`\"{}, and \textbackslash{}ref cmduntil \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}until\char`\"{} commands. An internal pointer is used for these commands. The \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}dontinclude \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} sets the pointer to the first line of the example. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a9addb372d91567fb4f4cc699337a7396}{par}} \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{Example\+:\textbackslash{}include}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_c_make_cache_8txt_a621773874dd04d298144e4ee887d4aea}{include.\+cpp}} Where the example \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_c_make_cache_8txt_a621773874dd04d298144e4ee887d4aea}{include\+\_\+test.\+cpp}} looks as \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{follows\+:\textbackslash{}include}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_c_make_cache_8txt_a621773874dd04d298144e4ee887d4aea}{include\+\_\+test.\+cpp}} \textbackslash{}htmlonly Click$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} href=\char`\"{}examples/\mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}}/html/pag\+\_\+example.\+html\char`\"{}$>$here$<$/\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} $>$ for the corresponding H\+T\+ML documentation that is generated by doxygen. \textbackslash{}endhtmlonly \textbackslash{}latexonly See \textbackslash{}hyperlink\{include\+\_\+example\}\{\mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2pre_8cpp_a0cf3fa621611a219b448ffbf42cafe00}{Include}} example\} for the corresponding \textbackslash{}mbox\{\textbackslash{}La\+TeX\} documentation that is generated by doxygen. \textbackslash{}endlatexonly \textbackslash{}sa sections \textbackslash{}ref cmdline \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}line\char`\"{}, \textbackslash{}ref cmdskip \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}skip\char`\"{}, \textbackslash{}ref cmdskipline \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}skipline\char`\"{}, \textbackslash{}ref cmduntil \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}until\char`\"{}, and \textbackslash{}ref cmdinclude \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}include\char`\"{}.$<$ hr $>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdinclude \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}\{ \textquotesingle{}option\textquotesingle{}\}\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}}-\/name $>$ \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} source \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} as \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} block of code. The \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} takes the name of an \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} as an argument. Source files or directories can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} specified using the \textbackslash{}ref cfg\+\_\+example\+\_\+path \char`\"{}E\+X\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH\char`\"{} tag of doxygen \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a011c73f2dbb87635a3b4206c72355f6e}{s}} configuration file. If \textbackslash{}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}}-\/name\textbackslash{}$>$ itself is not unique for the \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a71ce05caaf1d98a296e01c62ee8489b3}{set}} of example files specified by the \textbackslash{}ref cfg\+\_\+example\+\_\+path \char`\"{}E\+X\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH\char`\"{} tag, you can \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} part of the absolute path to disambiguate it. \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2scanner_8cpp_ac5b8a46397fb918912c84d402bc53484}{Using}} the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} is equivalent to inserting the \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} into the documentation block \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} surrounding it with \textbackslash{}ref cmdcode \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}code\char`\"{} and \textbackslash{}ref cmdendcode \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endcode\char`\"{} commands. The \mbox{\hyperlink{main_8cpp_ae66f6b31b5ad750f1fe042a706a4e3d4}{main}} purpose of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} is to avoid \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_a7ebb47cd48f4220dc255e5fea2063b89}{code}} duplication in case of example blocks that consist of multiple source \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} header files. For \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} line by line description of \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} source files use the \textbackslash{}ref cmddontinclude \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}dontinclude\char`\"{} command in combination with the \textbackslash{}ref cmdline \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}line\char`\"{}, \textbackslash{}ref cmdskip \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}skip\char`\"{}, \textbackslash{}ref cmdskipline \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}skipline\char`\"{}, and \textbackslash{}ref cmduntil \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}until\char`\"{} commands. Alternatively, the \textbackslash{}ref cmdsnippet \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}snippet\char`\"{} command can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} only \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} fragment of \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} source file. For \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad61af623360700a24d0f4b7682a029fb}{this}} to work the fragment has to \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} marked. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad0ca7f287bf31aee006876639e63bfcb}{note}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}} \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a011c73f2dbb87635a3b4206c72355f6e}{s}} special commands do not work inside blocks of code. It is allowed to nest \mbox{\hyperlink{class_c}{C}}-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a83adb69d9f54bfc92ceb3ceb6d965eb7}{style}} comments inside \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_a7ebb47cd48f4220dc255e5fea2063b89}{code}} block though. The \`{}option\`{} can either \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} \`{}lineno\`{} or \`{}\mbox{\hyperlink{vhdljjparser_8cpp_a9910424bf5401d657c3b3fdff6fcc152}{doc}}\`{}. The \`{}option\`{} \`{}lineno\`{} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to enable line numbers for the \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a327f3dad9da687756493417c1c902612}{included}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_a7ebb47cd48f4220dc255e5fea2063b89}{code}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} desired. The \`{}option\`{} \`{}\mbox{\hyperlink{vhdljjparser_8cpp_a9910424bf5401d657c3b3fdff6fcc152}{doc}}\`{} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to treat the \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} as documentation rather than code. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad0ca7f287bf31aee006876639e63bfcb}{note}} Some that when using the \`{}\{\mbox{\hyperlink{vhdljjparser_8cpp_a9910424bf5401d657c3b3fdff6fcc152}{doc}}\}\`{} option, commands like \textbackslash{}ref cmdcond \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}cond\char`\"{} and \textbackslash{}ref cmdif \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}if\char`\"{} don \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{058__bracket__recursion_8tcl_a69e959f6901827e4d8271aeaa5fba0fc}{t}} work with using \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_aea1b72c1122f23fa4924a7bcaf120f0a}{sizeindication}} = $<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a1e79fade784ffb450b103ad42e120fa0}{size}} $>$\mbox{]} \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}dot Starts \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} text fragment which should contain \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} valid description of \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} dot graph. The text fragment ends with \textbackslash{}ref cmdenddot \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}enddot\char`\"{}. Doxygen will pass the text on to dot \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} the resulting image(\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} image map) into the output. The first argument is optional \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to specify the caption that is displayed below the image. This argument has to \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} specified between quotes even \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} it does not contain any spaces. The quotes \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a8ed5a546d1a76d96eeab1587ee2de2c1}{are}} stripped before the caption is displayed. The second argument is also optional \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to specify the \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_aed511cafb3c2907e512720bcea22f627}{width}} or height of the image. For \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} description of the possibilities see the \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} \textbackslash{}ref image\+\_\+sizeindicator \char`\"{}Size indication\char`\"{} with the \textbackslash{}ref cmdimage \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}image\char`\"{} command. endcode$<$ hr $>$ section cmdemoji \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_aac5f64589f4ff20ecbf069115731c60c}{emoji}} name This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} will produce an \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_aac5f64589f4ff20ecbf069115731c60c}{emoji}} character given its name The supported names \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a8ed5a546d1a76d96eeab1587ee2de2c1}{are}} the ones also supported by Git\+Hub \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} listed here \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a8c90afd4641b25be86bd09983c3cbee0}{i}} \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_aff65a51a703804e0ad1adbcfd76c86f8}{e}} \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_aac5f64589f4ff20ecbf069115731c60c}{emoji}} smile is the same as \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_adb2dbc8c43288a024535ed507da7b278}{writing}} \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a8c90afd4641b25be86bd09983c3cbee0}{i}} \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_aff65a51a703804e0ad1adbcfd76c86f8}{e}} \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_aac5f64589f4ff20ecbf069115731c60c}{emoji}} unsupported will \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ab80390469f4ea47410f6308d3c889aab}{produce}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily using \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_aa48914cdbda20ebbc9d958e7d32c9797}{A\+L\+I\+A\+S\+ES}} =  \char`\"{}reminder=\textbackslash{}xrefitem reminders \textbackslash{}\char`\"{}Reminder\textbackslash{}\char`\"{} \textbackslash{}\char`\"{}Reminders\textbackslash{}\char`\"{}\char`\"{} \textbackslash{}endverbatim Note the use of escaped quotes for the second \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} third argument of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}xrefitem command. In case parameter \char`\"{}(heading)\char`\"{} is the empty \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a13690c1a2aacb1c8261e3be3c4a4f4b2}{string}} no heading is generated. This can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} useful when used in combination with the \textbackslash{}ref cmdpage \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}page\char`\"{} command e.\+g. \textbackslash{}verbatim \#define M\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+C\+A\+N\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+\_\+\+F\+I\+LE 101 \#define M\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+C\+A\+N\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+C\+L\+O\+S\+E\+\_\+\+F\+I\+LE 102 \textbackslash{}endverbatim with \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}error defined as \textbackslash{}verbatim \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_aa48914cdbda20ebbc9d958e7d32c9797}{A\+L\+I\+A\+S\+ES}} += \char`\"{}error=\textbackslash{}xrefitem my\+\_\+errors \textbackslash{}\char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\char`\"{} \textbackslash{}\char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\char`\"{}\char`\"{} \textbackslash{}endverbatim $<$hr$>$ $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdaddindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}addindex (text) \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}addindex This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} adds (text) to the \textbackslash{}La\+TeX , Doc\+Book \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} R\+TF index. $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdanchor \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}anchor $<$word$>$ \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}anchor This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} places an invisible, named anchor into the documentation to which you can refer with the \textbackslash{}ref cmdref \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ref\char`\"{} command. \textbackslash{}sa section \textbackslash{}ref cmdref \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ref\char`\"{}. $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdcite \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}cite $<$label$>$ \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}cite Adds \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} bibliographic reference in the text \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} in the list of bibliographic references. The \textbackslash{}$<$label\textbackslash{}$>$ must \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} valid Bib\+TeX label that can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} found in one of the .bib files listed in \textbackslash{}ref cfg\+\_\+cite\+\_\+bib\+\_\+files \char`\"{}C\+I\+T\+E\+\_\+\+B\+I\+B\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+ES\char`\"{}. For the \textbackslash{}La\+TeX \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad41edd103217aafc3fb5613fe98b87a0}{output}} the formatting of the reference in the text can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} configured with \textbackslash{}ref cfg\+\_\+latex\+\_\+bib\+\_\+style \char`\"{}L\+A\+T\+E\+X\+\_\+\+B\+I\+B\+\_\+\+S\+T\+Y\+LE\char`\"{}. For other \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad41edd103217aafc3fb5613fe98b87a0}{output}} formats \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} fixed representation is used. Note that using \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad61af623360700a24d0f4b7682a029fb}{this}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} requires the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} bibtex tool to \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} present in the \mbox{\hyperlink{search__functions_8php_af66786bda8b625ad1ea9c3e8adf0862f}{search}} path. $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdendlink \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endlink \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endlink This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} ends \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} link that is started with the \textbackslash{}ref cmdlink \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}link\char`\"{} command. \textbackslash{}sa section \textbackslash{}ref cmdlink \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}link\char`\"{}. $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdlink \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}link $<$link-\/object$>$ \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}link The links that \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a8ed5a546d1a76d96eeab1587ee2de2c1}{are}} automatically generated by doxygen always have the name of the object they point to as link-\/text. The \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}link \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to create \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} link to an object (\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}}, class, or member) with \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} user specified link-\/text. The link \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} should end with an \textbackslash{}ref cmdendlink \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endlink\char`\"{} command. All text between the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}link \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \textbackslash{}ref cmdendlink \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endlink\char`\"{} commands serves as text for \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} link to the \textbackslash{}$<$link-\/object\textbackslash{}$>$ specified as the first argument of \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}link. \textbackslash{}sa Section \textbackslash{}ref autolink \char`\"{}autolink\char`\"{} for more information on automatically generated links \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} valid link-\/objects. $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdref \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ref $<$name$>$ \mbox{[}\char`\"{}(text)\char`\"{}\mbox{]} \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ref Creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} reference to \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} named section, subsection, page or anchor. For H\+T\+ML documentation the reference \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} will generate \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} link to the section. For \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} section or subsection the title of the section will \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used as the text of the link. For an anchor the optional text between quotes will \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used or \textbackslash{}$<$name\textbackslash{}$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} no text is specified. For \textbackslash{}La\+TeX documentation the reference \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} will generate \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} section number for sections or the text followed by \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} page number \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} \textbackslash{}$<$name\textbackslash{}$>$ refers to an anchor. \textbackslash{}sa Section \textbackslash{}ref cmdpage \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}page\char`\"{} for an example of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ref command. $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdrefitem \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}refitem $<$name$>$ \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}refitem Just like the \textbackslash{}ref cmdref \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ref\char`\"{} command, \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad61af623360700a24d0f4b7682a029fb}{this}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} reference to \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} named section, but \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad61af623360700a24d0f4b7682a029fb}{this}} reference appears in \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} list that is started by \textbackslash{}ref cmdsecreflist \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}secreflist\char`\"{} and ends with \textbackslash{}ref cmdendsecreflist \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endsecreflist\char`\"{}. An example of such \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} list can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} seen \textbackslash{}ref showsecreflist \char`\"{}at the top of the page\char`\"{}. $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdsecreflist \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}secreflist \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}secreflist Starts an index list of item, created with \textbackslash{}ref cmdrefitem \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}refitem\char`\"{} that each link to \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} named section. $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdendsecreflist \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endsecreflist \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endsecreflist \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2vhdlcode_8cpp_a342404d3b71fbd50588f779f1f1c59b3}{End}} an index list started with \textbackslash{}ref cmdsecreflist \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}secreflist\char`\"{}. $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdsubpage \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subpage $<$name$>$ \mbox{[}\char`\"{}(text)\char`\"{}\mbox{]} \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subpage This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to create \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} hierarchy of pages. The same structure can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} made using the \textbackslash{}ref cmddefgroup \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}defgroup\char`\"{} and \textbackslash{}ref cmdingroup \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ingroup\char`\"{} commands, but for pages the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subpage \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} is often more convenient. The \mbox{\hyperlink{main_8cpp_ae66f6b31b5ad750f1fe042a706a4e3d4}{main}} page (see \textbackslash{}ref cmdmainpage \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}mainpage\char`\"{}) is typically the root of hierarchy. This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} behaves similar as \textbackslash{}ref cmdref \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ref\char`\"{} in the sense that it creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} reference to \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} page labeled \textbackslash{}$<$name\textbackslash{}$>$ with the optional link text as specified in the second argument. It differs from the \textbackslash{}ref cmdref \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}ref\char`\"{} command in that it only works for pages, \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} parent-\/child relation between pages, where the child page (or \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_acc128504834a67c06b246c155ca48807}{sub}} page) is identified by label \textbackslash{}$<$name\textbackslash{}$>$. See the \textbackslash{}ref cmdsection \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}section\char`\"{} and \textbackslash{}ref cmdsubsection \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsection\char`\"{} commands \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} you want to \mbox{\hyperlink{restypedef_8cpp_a102acaaa258e937adf910898c6133545}{add}} structure without creating multiple pages. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad0ca7f287bf31aee006876639e63bfcb}{note}} Each page can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} the \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_acc128504834a67c06b246c155ca48807}{sub}} page of only one other page \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} no cyclic relations \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a8ed5a546d1a76d96eeab1587ee2de2c1}{are}} allowed, i.\+e. the page hierarchy must have \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} tree structure. Here is an example\+: \textbackslash{}verbatim \textbackslash{}endverbatim $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdtableofcontents \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}tableofcontents\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}\{\textquotesingle{}\mbox{[}option\mbox{[}\+:\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}}\mbox{]}\mbox{]}\mbox{[},option\mbox{[}\+:\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}}\mbox{]}\mbox{]}$\ast$\textquotesingle{}\}\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}tableofcontents Creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} table of contents at the top of \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} page, listing all sections \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} subsections in the page. The \`{}option\`{} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} \`{}H\+T\+ML\`{} or \`{}La\+TeX\`{} or \`{}X\+ML\`{} or \`{}Doc\+Book\`{}. When \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} \`{}\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}}\`{} is specified \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad61af623360700a24d0f4b7682a029fb}{this}} means the maximum nesting \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}} that is shown. The value of \`{}\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}}\`{} should \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} in the range 1..\+5, \mbox{\hyperlink{qtextcodec_8cpp_a48ca6217f9d5d1de9776060e1a8dbe58}{values}} outside \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad61af623360700a24d0f4b7682a029fb}{this}} range \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a8ed5a546d1a76d96eeab1587ee2de2c1}{are}} considered to \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} 5. In case no \`{}\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}}\`{} is specified \`{}\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}}\`{} is \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a71ce05caaf1d98a296e01c62ee8489b3}{set}} to 5 (show all) In case no \`{}option\`{}. is specified \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}tableofcontents acts as \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} just the \`{}option\`{} \`{}H\+T\+ML\`{} \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \`{}X\+ML\`{} was specified. In case of multiple \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}tableofcontents commands in \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} page the \`{}option\`{}(\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a011c73f2dbb87635a3b4206c72355f6e}{s}}) will \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used additional to the already specified \`{}option\`{}(\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a011c73f2dbb87635a3b4206c72355f6e}{s}}), but only the last \`{}\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a68fa175816cc25c7c9ea3553ea2aab98}{level}}\`{} of an \`{}option\`{} is valid. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{qglobal_8h_ac3b81b0c037874b7fcfd69376a6d5594}{warning}} This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} only works inside related page documentation \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_aff65a51a703804e0ad1adbcfd76c86f8}{e}} not in other documentation blocks \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} only has effect in the the specified output! $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdsection \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}section $<$section-\/name$>$ (section title) \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}section Creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} section with name \textbackslash{}$<$section-\/name\textbackslash{}$>$. The title of the section should \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} specified as the second argument of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}section command. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{qglobal_8h_ac3b81b0c037874b7fcfd69376a6d5594}{warning}} This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} only works inside related page documentation \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_aff65a51a703804e0ad1adbcfd76c86f8}{e}} not in other documentation blocks! \textbackslash{}sa Section \textbackslash{}ref cmdpage \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}page\char`\"{} for an example of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}section command. $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdsubsection \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsection $<$subsection-\/name$>$ (subsection title) \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsection Creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} subsection with name \textbackslash{}$<$subsection-\/name\textbackslash{}$>$. The title of the subsection should \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} specified as the second argument of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsection command. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{qglobal_8h_ac3b81b0c037874b7fcfd69376a6d5594}{warning}} This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} only works inside \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} section of \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} related page documentation block \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_aff65a51a703804e0ad1adbcfd76c86f8}{e}} not in other documentation blocks! \textbackslash{}sa Section \textbackslash{}ref cmdpage \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}page\char`\"{} for an example of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsection command. $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdsubsubsection \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsubsection $<$subsubsection-\/name$>$ (subsubsection title) \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsubsection Creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} subsubsection with name \textbackslash{}$<$subsubsection-\/name\textbackslash{}$>$. The title of the subsubsection should \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} specified as the second argument of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsubsection command. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{qglobal_8h_ac3b81b0c037874b7fcfd69376a6d5594}{warning}} This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} only works inside \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} subsection of \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} related page documentation block \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_aff65a51a703804e0ad1adbcfd76c86f8}{e}} not in other documentation blocks! \textbackslash{}sa Section \textbackslash{}ref cmdpage \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}page\char`\"{} for an example of the \textbackslash{}ref cmdsection \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}section\char`\"{} command \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \textbackslash{}ref cmdsubsection \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}subsection\char`\"{} command. $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdparagraph \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} $<$\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}}-\/name$>$ (\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} title) \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} Creates \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} named \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} with name \textbackslash{}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}}-\/name\textbackslash{}$>$. The title of the \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} should \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} specified as the second argument of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} command. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{qglobal_8h_ac3b81b0c037874b7fcfd69376a6d5594}{warning}} This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} only works inside \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} subsubsection of \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} related page documentation block \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_aff65a51a703804e0ad1adbcfd76c86f8}{e}} not in other documentation blocks! $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}htmlonly$<$/\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a15229b450f26d8fa1c10bea4f3279f4d}{p}}$>$$<$center$>$$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a15229b450f26d8fa1c10bea4f3279f4d}{p}}$>$\textbackslash{}endhtmlonly $<$h2$>$ \textbackslash{}htmlonly -\/-\/-\/ \textbackslash{}endhtmlonly Commands for displaying examples \textbackslash{}htmlonly -\/-\/-\/ \textbackslash{}endhtmlonly $<$/h2$>$ \textbackslash{}htmlonly$<$/\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a15229b450f26d8fa1c10bea4f3279f4d}{p}}$>$$<$/center$>$$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a15229b450f26d8fa1c10bea4f3279f4d}{p}}$>$\textbackslash{}endhtmlonly $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmddontinclude \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}dontinclude\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}\{lineno\}\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} $<$\mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}}-\/name$>$ \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}dontinclude This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a8ac09b377c3e2343a4bf758132f67c22}{parse}} \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} source \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} without actually verbatim including it in the documentation (as the \textbackslash{}ref cmdinclude \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}include\char`\"{} command does). This is useful \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} you want to divide the source \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} into smaller pieces \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \mbox{\hyperlink{restypedef_8cpp_a102acaaa258e937adf910898c6133545}{add}} documentation between the pieces. Source files or directories can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} specified using the \textbackslash{}ref cfg\+\_\+example\+\_\+path \char`\"{}E\+X\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH\char`\"{} tag of doxygen\textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a011c73f2dbb87635a3b4206c72355f6e}{s}} configuration file. You can \mbox{\hyperlink{restypedef_8cpp_a102acaaa258e937adf910898c6133545}{add}} option \`{}\{lineno\}\`{} to enable line numbers for the \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a327f3dad9da687756493417c1c902612}{included}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_a7ebb47cd48f4220dc255e5fea2063b89}{code}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} desired. The class \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} member declarations \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} definitions inside the \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_a7ebb47cd48f4220dc255e5fea2063b89}{code}} fragment \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a8ed5a546d1a76d96eeab1587ee2de2c1}{are}} \textquotesingle{}remembered\textquotesingle{} during the parsing of the \mbox{\hyperlink{vhdldocgen_8cpp_ae8c2c4e6dab650ca0dbc32956838ddd9}{comment}} block that contained the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}dontinclude command. For line by line descriptions of source files, one or more lines of the example can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} displayed using the \textbackslash{}ref cmdline \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}line\char`\"{}, \textbackslash{}ref cmdskip \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}skip\char`\"{}, \textbackslash{}ref cmdskipline \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}skipline\char`\"{}, and \textbackslash{}ref cmduntil \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}until\char`\"{} commands. An internal pointer is used for these commands. The \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}dontinclude \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} sets the pointer to the first line of the example. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a9addb372d91567fb4f4cc699337a7396}{par}} Example\+: \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_c_make_cache_8txt_a621773874dd04d298144e4ee887d4aea}{include.\+cpp}} Where the example \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_c_make_cache_8txt_a621773874dd04d298144e4ee887d4aea}{include\+\_\+test.\+cpp}} looks as follows\+: \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_c_make_cache_8txt_a621773874dd04d298144e4ee887d4aea}{include\+\_\+test.\+cpp}} \textbackslash{}htmlonly Click $<$\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} href=\char`\"{}examples/\mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}}/html/pag\+\_\+example.\+html\char`\"{}$>$here$<$/\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}}$>$ for the corresponding H\+T\+ML documentation that is generated by doxygen. \textbackslash{}endhtmlonly \textbackslash{}latexonly See \textbackslash{}hyperlink\{include\+\_\+example\}\{\mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2pre_8cpp_a0cf3fa621611a219b448ffbf42cafe00}{Include}} example\} for the corresponding \textbackslash{}mbox\{\textbackslash{}La\+TeX\} documentation that is generated by doxygen. \textbackslash{}endlatexonly \textbackslash{}sa sections \textbackslash{}ref cmdline \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}line\char`\"{}, \textbackslash{}ref cmdskip \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}skip\char`\"{}, \textbackslash{}ref cmdskipline \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}skipline\char`\"{}, \textbackslash{}ref cmduntil \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}until\char`\"{}, and \textbackslash{}ref cmdinclude \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}include\char`\"{}. $<$hr$>$ \textbackslash{}section cmdinclude \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}\{\textquotesingle{}option\textquotesingle{}\}\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} $<$\mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}}-\/name$>$ \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} This \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} source \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} as \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} block of code. The \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} takes the name of an \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} as an argument. Source files or directories can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} specified using the \textbackslash{}ref cfg\+\_\+example\+\_\+path \char`\"{}E\+X\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH\char`\"{} tag of doxygen\textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a011c73f2dbb87635a3b4206c72355f6e}{s}} configuration file. If \textbackslash{}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}}-\/name\textbackslash{}$>$ itself is not unique for the \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a71ce05caaf1d98a296e01c62ee8489b3}{set}} of example files specified by the \textbackslash{}ref cfg\+\_\+example\+\_\+path \char`\"{}E\+X\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH\char`\"{} tag, you can \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} part of the absolute path to disambiguate it. \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2scanner_8cpp_ac5b8a46397fb918912c84d402bc53484}{Using}} the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} is equivalent to inserting the \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} into the documentation block \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} surrounding it with \textbackslash{}ref cmdcode \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}code\char`\"{} and \textbackslash{}ref cmdendcode \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}endcode\char`\"{} commands. The \mbox{\hyperlink{main_8cpp_ae66f6b31b5ad750f1fe042a706a4e3d4}{main}} purpose of the \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} is to avoid \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_a7ebb47cd48f4220dc255e5fea2063b89}{code}} duplication in case of example blocks that consist of multiple source \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} header files. For \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} line by line description of \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} source files use the \textbackslash{}ref cmddontinclude \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}dontinclude\char`\"{} command in combination with the \textbackslash{}ref cmdline \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}line\char`\"{}, \textbackslash{}ref cmdskip \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}skip\char`\"{}, \textbackslash{}ref cmdskipline \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}skipline\char`\"{}, and \textbackslash{}ref cmduntil \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}until\char`\"{} commands. Alternatively, the \textbackslash{}ref cmdsnippet \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}snippet\char`\"{} command can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} only \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} fragment of \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} source file. For \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad61af623360700a24d0f4b7682a029fb}{this}} to work the fragment has to \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} marked. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad0ca7f287bf31aee006876639e63bfcb}{note}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doxygen}{Doxygen}}\textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_a011c73f2dbb87635a3b4206c72355f6e}{s}} special commands do not work inside blocks of code. It is allowed to nest \mbox{\hyperlink{class_c}{C}}-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a83adb69d9f54bfc92ceb3ceb6d965eb7}{style}} comments inside \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_a7ebb47cd48f4220dc255e5fea2063b89}{code}} block though. The \`{}option\`{} can either \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} \`{}lineno\`{} or \`{}\mbox{\hyperlink{vhdljjparser_8cpp_a9910424bf5401d657c3b3fdff6fcc152}{doc}}\`{}. The \`{}option\`{} \`{}lineno\`{} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to enable line numbers for the \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a327f3dad9da687756493417c1c902612}{included}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_a7ebb47cd48f4220dc255e5fea2063b89}{code}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} desired. The \`{}option\`{} \`{}\mbox{\hyperlink{vhdljjparser_8cpp_a9910424bf5401d657c3b3fdff6fcc152}{doc}}\`{} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to treat the \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} as documentation rather than code. \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad0ca7f287bf31aee006876639e63bfcb}{note}} Some that when using the \`{}\{\mbox{\hyperlink{vhdljjparser_8cpp_a9910424bf5401d657c3b3fdff6fcc152}{doc}}\}\`{} option, commands like \textbackslash{}ref cmdcond \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}cond\char`\"{} and \textbackslash{}ref cmdif \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}if\char`\"{} don\textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{058__bracket__recursion_8tcl_a69e959f6901827e4d8271aeaa5fba0fc}{t}} work with \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad61af623360700a24d0f4b7682a029fb}{this}} \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} due to the moment of parsing. For example, the putting the following \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2tclscanner_8cpp_ad732c0c7a8bcc3ecf8c7c360b382740d}{command}} in the documentation, references \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} snippet in \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab14f56bc3bd7680490ece4ad7815465f}{c}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_c_make_cache_8txt_a621773874dd04d298144e4ee887d4aea}{example.\+cpp}} residing in \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} subdirectory which should \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} pointed to by \textbackslash{}ref cfg\+\_\+example\+\_\+path \char`\"{}E\+X\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH\char`\"{}. \textbackslash{}verbatim \textbackslash{}snippet snippets/\mbox{\hyperlink{_c_make_cache_8txt_a621773874dd04d298144e4ee887d4aea}{example.\+cpp}} Adding \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} resource \textbackslash{}endverbatim The text following the \mbox{\hyperlink{examples_2_c_make_lists_8txt_a23c022ca6bc91151baee0c9eb0907f12}{file}} name is the unique identifier for the snippet.
