\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sizeindication}{sizeindication}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily using \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_aea1b72c1122f23fa4924a7bcaf120f0a}{sizeindication}} =  $<$\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a1e79fade784ffb450b103ad42e120fa0}{size}}$>$\mbox{]} \textbackslash{}addindex \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}dot Starts \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} text fragment which should contain \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} valid description of \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} dot graph. The text fragment ends with \textbackslash{}ref cmdenddot \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}enddot\char`\"{}. Doxygen will pass the text on to dot \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} \mbox{\hyperlink{libversion_2_c_make_lists_8txt_af0600ec3a126074ad09791f1307fd359}{include}} the resulting image (\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} image map) into the output. The first argument is optional \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to specify the caption that is displayed below the image. This argument has to \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} specified between quotes even \mbox{\hyperlink{generated__src_2xmlcode_8cpp_ad4a65b873df5c05570846b5413b41dfd}{if}} it does not contain any spaces. The quotes \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a8ed5a546d1a76d96eeab1587ee2de2c1}{are}} stripped before the caption is displayed. The second argument is also optional \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad4c2a920586fa780cac1476ec08702e1}{and}} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used to specify the \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_aed511cafb3c2907e512720bcea22f627}{width}} or height of the image. For \mbox{\hyperlink{060__command__switch_8tcl_ab08ae027fc5777bc4f0629f1b60b35db}{a}} description of the possibilities see the \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} \textbackslash{}ref image\+\_\+sizeindicator \char`\"{}Size indication\char`\"{} with the \textbackslash{}ref cmdimage \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}image\char`\"{} command. \DoxyCodeLine{\{ exception description \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \(\backslash\)addindex \(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)exception}
\DoxyCodeLine{  Starts an exception description \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} an exception \textcolor{keywordtype}{object} with name}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \(\backslash\)<exception-\/\textcolor{keywordtype}{object}\(\backslash\)>. Followed by \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_ae1c02e9f36a12e377487affe87df4bb6}{a}} description of the exception.}
\DoxyCodeLine{  The existence of the exception \textcolor{keywordtype}{object} is not checked.}
\DoxyCodeLine{  The text of the \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} has no special \textcolor{keyword}{internal} structure. All visual}
\DoxyCodeLine{  enhancement commands may \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used inside the \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{  Multiple \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a4e1e0e72dd773439e333c84dd762a9c3}{adjacent \(\backslash\)c}} \(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)exception commands will \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} joined into \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_ae1c02e9f36a12e377487affe87df4bb6}{a}} single \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{  Each exception description will start on \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_ae1c02e9f36a12e377487affe87df4bb6}{a}} \textcolor{keyword}{new} line.}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a4e1e0e72dd773439e333c84dd762a9c3}{The \(\backslash\)c}} \(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)exception description ends when \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_ae1c02e9f36a12e377487affe87df4bb6}{a}} blank line or some other}
\DoxyCodeLine{  sectioning \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a0427896be3612bb482dc4829ed16b8d7}{command}} is encountered. See section \(\backslash\)ref cmdfn \textcolor{stringliteral}{"\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)fn"} \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} an}
\DoxyCodeLine{  example.}

\DoxyCodeLine{  Starts \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_ae1c02e9f36a12e377487affe87df4bb6}{a}} \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} where \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_ae1c02e9f36a12e377487affe87df4bb6}{a}} \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad0ca7f287bf31aee006876639e63bfcb}{note}} can \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} entered. The \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} will \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  indented. The text of the \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}} has no special \textcolor{keyword}{internal} structure.}
\DoxyCodeLine{  All visual enhancement commands may \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} used inside the \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{  Multiple \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_a4e1e0e72dd773439e333c84dd762a9c3}{adjacent \(\backslash\)c}} \(\backslash\)\mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad0ca7f287bf31aee006876639e63bfcb}{\(\backslash\)note}} commands will \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_af0bf8322edf25090b1a3ef7e10cc30d1}{be}} joined into \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_ae1c02e9f36a12e377487affe87df4bb6}{a}} single \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_a5acd1ad7c97cfecf909a8536819ca933}{paragraph}}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{  Each \mbox{\hyperlink{commands_8doc_ad0ca7f287bf31aee006876639e63bfcb}{note}} description will start on \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8h_ae1c02e9f36a12e377487affe87df4bb6}{a}} \textcolor{keyword}{new} line.}
\DoxyCodeLine{  Alternatively}

\end{DoxyCode}
